BUSINESS GENERAL Sunbeam Corporation (collectively subsidiaries, "Company" "Sunbeam") leading designer, manufacturer marketer branded consumer products. The Company's primary business manufacture, marketing distribution durable household consumer products mass market distributors United States internationally. The Company sells products commercial end users hotels institutions (the "Away From Home" category business). The Company's product categories are: (1) Appliances (mixers, blenders, food steamers, bread makers, rice cookers, coffee makers, toasters, irons garment steamers) (2) Health Home (vaporizers, humidifiers, air cleaners, water filters, massagers, hot cold packs, blood pressure monitors scales) (3) Personal Care Comfort (shower massagers, hair clippers trimmers, electric warming blankets throws) (4) Outdoor Cooking (electric, gas charcoal grills grill accessories) (5) Away From Home (clippers related products professional beauty, barber veterinarian trade sales products commercial institutional channels). The International Group responsible sales (primarily small appliances, personal care, grills comfort products, professional clippers related products) countries United States. Sunbeam products enjoy long-standing reputation quality, majority Company's sales products hold number market share respective product categories. The Company organized 1989 (as Sunbeam-Oster Company, Inc.) September 1990, Sunbeam acquired assets assumed liabilities, reorganization, Allegheny International, Inc. (the "Predecessor"), entity operating debtor-in-possession Chapter 11 United States Bankruptcy Code 1988. In August 1992, Company completed public offering 20,000,000 shares common stock. In May 1995, Company changed Sunbeam-Oster Company, Inc. Sunbeam Corporation. RESTRUCTURING GROWTH PLAN In Fall 1996, newly elected Chairman, Albert J. Dunlap, Company announced major restructuring growth plan. The restructuring portion plan completed 1997, resulting significant reduction employees, facilities costs, anticipated generate approximately $225 million annual savings Company. As part restructuring plan, Company divested non-core businesses assets, including furniture, time temperature, decorative bedding, gas heaters logs, Counselor/registered trademark/ Borg/registered trademark/ scale businesses Company's Biddeford, Maine textile mill. The Company's restructuring plan included closure 18 factories, 43 warehouses 5 headquarters, resulting consolidation corporate offices single headquarters office located Delray Beach, Florida operations center Hattiesburg manufacturing distribution facility. The number manufacturing facilities reduced twenty-six (four US international). See "Properties" below. The Company consolidated purchasing functions, substantially reduced number stock keeping units maintained Company outsourced administrative, manufacturing distribution activities. The Company developed comprehensive year growth plan core businesses. Sunbeam's goal revenues double, reaching $2 billion 1999, operating margins improving 1 <PAGE> 20% sales. This revenue growth anticipated derived, large part, development innovative products globalization Company. Domestically, goal introduce 30 products year; 1997, Company introduced 35 domestic products 54 international products. In international business, Company goal triple international sales $600 million 1999. During 1997 Company entered 25 international distribution/license agreements. The Company identified channels distribution additional sales growth opportunities, including commercial organizations "direct consumer" channels catalogs, Internet Sunbeam/registered trademark/ factory outlet stores. These growth plans reflect impact Company's pending acquisitions The Coleman Company, Inc., Signature Brands USA, Inc. First Alert, Inc. See "PENDING ACQUISITIONS". Both international expansion product introductions supported significant investment major advertising program geared continually strengthening Sunbeam/registered trademark/, Oster/registered trademark/, Grillmaster/registered trademark/ brands marketplace. PENDING ACQUISITIONS On March 2, 1998, Company announced entered separate agreements acquire The Coleman Company, Inc., Signature Brands USA, Inc. First Alert, Inc. ("Coleman"), 1997 revenues approximately $1.1 billion, world's leading manufacturer marketer outdoor recreational products. It manufactures distributes widely diversified product lines camping, leisure time hardware markets, Coleman/registered trademark/, Powermate/registered trademark/, Camping Gaz/registered trademark/ Eastpak/registered trademark/ brand names. The Coleman transaction valued approximately $2.0 billion, consisting approximately $811 million Company common stock, approximately $260 million cash assumption debt. Signature Brands USA, Inc. ("Signature Brands"), 1997 revenues approximately $279 million, leading manufacturer comprehensive line consumer professional products, including coffee makers marketed Mr. Coffee/registered trademark/ brand consumer health products marketed Health-o-Meter/registered trademark/, Counselor/registered trademark/ Borg/registered trademark/ brand names. The Signature Brands transaction valued approximately $250 million, consisting cash assumption debt. First Alert, Inc. ("First Alert"), revenues approximately $187 million, worldwide leader residential safety equipment including smoke carbon monoxide detectors marketed First Alert/registered trademark/ brand name. The First Alert transaction valued approximately $175 million, consisting cash assumption debt. In connection transactions, Company intends seek negotiate bank credit facility issue debt securities. MANAGEMENT'S DISCUSSION ANALYSIS FINANCIAL CONDITION RESULTS OPERATION ENDED 28, 1997 COMPARED ENDED 29, 1996 In November 1996, Company initiated major restructuring growth plan designed substantially reduce cost structure grow business order restore higher levels profitability Company. By July 1997, Company completed major phases restructuring plan. The $225.0 million annualized cost savings anticipated restructuring results primarily consolidation administrative functions Company, rationalization manufacturing warehouse facilities (including reduction number production facilities 26 8 warehouses 61 18), elimination 6,000 positions (including 3,300 divestiture non-core businesses approximately 2,800 positions), centralization Company's procurement function re-negotiation supply contracts resulting procurement savings raw materials, components sourced finished products reduction Company's product offerings stock keeping units ("SKU's"). The restructuring growth plan included redefinition Company's core product categories elimination businesses product lines fit core categories. Sunbeam's core product categories Appliances, Health Home, Personal Care Comfort, Outdoor Cooking Away From Home. Product categories businesses determined non-core divested 1997, including Company's furniture business time temperature, decorative bedding Counselor/registered trademark/ Borg/registered trademark/ scale product lines. In addition, Company sold textile mill Biddeford, Maine 1997. Net sales continuing operations 1997 $1,168.2 million, increase $183.9 million 18.7% 1996. Net sales normalized basis, excluding divested product lines classified discontinued operations (time temperature products, decorative bedding Counselor/registered trademark/ Borg/registered trademark/ branded scales), increased 22.4% year. Global sales, normalized basis, increased 1997 Company's product categories primarily product introductions, improved distribution (particularly Company's top ten customers), international geographic expansion improved price realization products. Global sales growth normalized basis exceeded 25% Appliance, Outdoor Cooking Away From Home categories sales increases 26.8%, 27.2% 28.6%, respectively. OPERATIONS SIGNIFICANT ACCOUNTING POLICIES ORGANIZATION Sunbeam Corporation ("Sunbeam" "Company") leading manufacturer marketer branded consumer products. The Sunbeam/registered trademark/ Oster/registered trademark/ brands household names generations, Company market share leader product categories. The Company markets products virtually category retailer including mass merchandisers, catalog showrooms, warehouse clubs, department stores, catalogs, television shopping channels, Company-owned outlet stores, hardware stores, home centers, drug grocery stores, pet supply retailers, independent distributors military. The Company sells products commercial end users hotels institutions. Approximately 79% total Company sales generated United States. The remaining sales generated primarily Latin America, Mexico, Canada, Europe Asia. PRINCIPLES CONSOLIDATION The consolidated financial statements include accounts Company majority-owned subsidiaries controls. All material intercompany balances transactions eliminated. PRESENTATION FISCAL PERIODS The Company's fiscal year ends Sunday nearest December 31. Fiscal years 1997, 1996 1995 ended December 28, 1997, December 29, 1996, December 31, 1995 respectively, encompassed 52-week periods. USE ESTIMATES The preparation consolidated financial statements conformity generally accepted accounting principles requires management make estimates assumptions affect amounts reported consolidated financial statements accompanying notes. Actual results differ estimates. Significant accounting estimates include establishment allowance doubtful accounts, reserves product warranty, product liability, excess obsolete inventory, litigation environmental exposures. CONCENTRATIONS CREDIT RISK Substantially Company's trade receivables due retailers distributors located United States, Latin America Canada. Approximately 36% Company's sales 1997 largest customers. The Company establishes credit policies based ongoing evaluation customers' creditworthiness competitive market conditions establishes allowance doubtful accounts based assessment exposures credit losses balance sheet date. The Company believes allowance doubtful accounts sufficient based credit exposures outstanding December 28, 1997. However, retailers filed bankruptcy protection years additional credit losses incurred trends retail consolidation continue. In addition, Company pays annual facility fee (currently .25%). The Credit Agreement financial covenants.
